\endhead
{\ttfamily -\/\#\#\#}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Print (but do not run) the commands to run for this compilation}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/-\/analyzer-\/output \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}value\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Static analyzer report output format (html\textbackslash{}$\vert$plist\textbackslash{}$\vert$plist-\/multi-\/file\textbackslash{}$\vert$plist-\/html\textbackslash{}$\vert$sarif\textbackslash{}$\vert$text).}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/-\/analyze}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Run the static analyzer}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/arcmt-\/migrate-\/emit-\/errors}   &Unsupported   &{\ttfamily Emit ARC errors even if the migrator can fix them}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/arcmt-\/migrate-\/report-\/output \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}value\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}   &Unsupported   &{\ttfamily Output path for the plist report}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/byteswapio}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Swap byte-\/order for unformatted input/output}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/B \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}dir\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Add \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}dir\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} to search path for binaries and object files used implicitly}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/CC}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Include comments from within macros in preprocessed output}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/denorms-\/are-\/zero}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Allow denormals to be flushed to zero.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/fast-\/relaxed-\/math}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Sets -\/cl-\/finite-\/math-\/only and -\/cl-\/unsafe-\/math-\/optimizations, and defines \+\_\+\+\_\+\+FAST\+\_\+\+RELAXED\+\_\+\+MATH\+\_\+\+\_\+.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/finite-\/math-\/only}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Allow floating-\/point optimizations that assume arguments and results are not Na\+Ns or +-\/Inf.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/fp32-\/correctly-\/rounded-\/divide-\/sqrt}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Specify that single precision floating-\/point divide and sqrt used in the program source are correctly rounded.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/kernel-\/arg-\/info}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Generate kernel argument metadata.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/mad-\/enable}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Allow use of less precise MAD computations in the generated binary.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/no-\/signed-\/zeros}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Allow use of less precise no signed zeros computations in the generated binary.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/opt-\/disable}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. This option disables all optimizations. By default optimizations are enabled.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/single-\/precision-\/constant}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Treat double precision floating-\/point constant as single precision constant.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/std=\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}value\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL language standard to compile for.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/strict-\/aliasing}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. This option is added for compatibility with Open\+CL 1.\+0.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/uniform-\/work-\/group-\/size}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Defines that the global work-\/size be a multiple of the work-\/group size specified to cl\+Enqueue\+NDRange\+Kernel}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/cl-\/unsafe-\/math-\/optimizations}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Open\+CL only. Allow unsafe floating-\/point optimizations. Also implies -\/cl-\/no-\/signed-\/zeros and -\/cl-\/mad-\/enable.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/-\/config \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}value\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Specifies configuration file}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/-\/cuda-\/compile-\/host-\/device}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Compile CUDA code for both host and device (default). Has no effect on non-\/\+CUDA compilations.}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/-\/cuda-\/device-\/only}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Compile CUDA code for device only}    \\\cline{1-3}
{\ttfamily -\/-\/cuda-\/host-\/only}   &Supported   &{\ttfamily Compile CUDA code for host only. Has no effect on non-\/\+CUDA compilations.}    \\\cline{1-3}

This uses a loose heuristic which considers functions vulnerable if they contain a char (or 8bit integer) array or constant sized calls to alloca , which are of greater size than ssp-\/buffer-\/size (default\+: 8 bytes). All variable sized calls to alloca are considered vulnerable. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} function with a stack protector has a guard value added to the stack frame that is checked on function exit. The guard value must be positioned in the stack frame such that a buffer overflow from a vulnerable variable will overwrite the guard value before overwriting the function\textquotesingle{}s return address. The reference stack guard value is stored in a global variable.{\ttfamily \textbackslash{}ilinebr \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}/td\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}/tr\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}
